id="17-frequently-asked-questions-1"><span data-lexical-text="true">Frequently Asked Questions</span></h3><h4 class="x1i97zcw x2klb21 xqui205" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">How do I Know Which Stat to Focus on?</span></h4><p class="x1f3rem xirccme xw7yly9" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">Check out </span><a href="https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1-QXvyDp0HjC01SRQGUmplTCK_n3eYeFY9AzJEE_QvEs/edit?gid=0#gid=0" target="_blank" rel="ugc nofollow noopener noreferrer" class="x1hl2dhg x1coeszu x1277o0a x5q9ga8" dir="ltr"><strong class="x117nqv4" data-lexical-text="true">My Sheet</strong></a><span data-lexical-text="true"> to balance our your Stats!</span></p><h4 class="x1i97zcw x2klb21 xqui205" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">Attack Speed Breakpoints</span></h4><p class="x1f3rem xirccme xw7yly9" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">Because the game's server operates in </span><em class="x1k4tb9n" data-lexical-text="true">frames</em><span data-lexical-text="true"> (images), Skills can only be cast in a whole number of frames. This means, for example, that you can't cast a Skill in 10.2 frames. To extend this example further, that means that all Attack Speed values that lead to a cast time of 10.01 to 10.99 frames would mean you end up casting at 11 frames, effectively wasting all Attack Speed gains from 11 frames to 10.01.</span><br><br><span data-lexical-text="true">For that reason, it is important to reach the Attack Speed Breakpoint of a frame.</span></p><p class="x1f3rem xirccme xw7yly9" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">You might be wondering how frames translate into actual Cast Speed. Because the server runs at 60 frames per second, the way we translate frames into Cast Speed is with the formula: 60 / Frames = Casts per Second.</span></p><h4 class="x1i97zcw x2klb21 xqui205" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">Breakpoints:</span></h4><p class="x1f3rem xirccme xw7yly9" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">Not found yet.</span></p><h4 class="x1i97zcw x2klb21 xqui205" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">Masterworking and Greater Affixes Explained</span></h4><p class="x1f3rem xirccme xw7yly9" dir="ltr"><span data-lexical-text="true">To find everything you need to know about Masterworking and Greater Affixes make sure to check our </span><a href="/diablo-4/guides/tempering-masterworking-guide" target="_blank" class="x1hl2dhg x1coeszu x1277o0a x5q9ga8" dir="ltr"><strong class="x117nqv4" data-lexical-text="true">Tempering and Masterworking Guide</strong></a><span data-lexical-text="true"> out.</span></p><h4 class="x1i97zcw x2klb21 xqui205"
